**GT:** `-1.1449635767559*x*exp(-Abs(x)) - 0.445567501246416*log(Abs(v) + 1) + 0.10853689295113*sin(t)`

The GT has three terms:
1. A term proportional to `x*exp(-|x|)` (depends on x only)
2. A term proportional to `log(|v| + 1)` (depends on v only)
3. A term proportional to `sin(t)` (depends on t only)

Key observations about what a candidate needs:
- **x-dependence**: `x*exp(-|x|)` — this is NOT `tanh(cx)`, NOT `x`, NOT `log(x²+1)`. The function `tanh` is fundamentally different from `x*exp(-|x|)`.
- **v-dependence**: `log(|v| + 1)` — this is NOT linear in v.
- **t-dependence**: `sin(t)` — straightforward.

Let me check if `tanh(c1*x)` could approximate `x*exp(-|x|)` for all x. The function `tanh(cx)` is an odd function bounded between -1 and 1, monotonically increasing. But `x*exp(-|x|)` is also odd, reaches a maximum at x=1, then decays to 0. These are fundamentally different — `tanh` approaches ±1 asymptotically while `x*exp(-|x|)` approaches 0. No choice of constants makes them equal for all x. Similarly, `tanh(c1*x + c2)` cannot match it either (unless c2 shifts, but that breaks the odd symmetry and still can't match the decay).

No combination of `tanh(c1*x + c2) + c*x` can match `x*exp(-|x|)` either, since for large |x|, tanh approaches ±1 and c*x grows linearly, while `x*exp(-|x|)` decays.

Similarly, `tanh(c1*x + c2) + c*x + c*log(c*x² + 1)` — none of these terms decay like `x*exp(-|x|)`.

For the v-dependence, `log(|v| + 1)` is nonlinear. Candidates with just `c*v` (linear in v) cannot match this. Candidates would need `log(...)` involving v, or `exp(c*v)`, or `v**c`, etc.

Looking at candidates with nonlinear v-dependence:
- **#13**: has `exp(c6*v)` — but `exp(cv)` cannot equal `log(|v|+1)` for all v.
- **#42**: has `v*|v|^(1/3)` — not `log(|v|+1)`.
- **#46**: has `v*log(c9*t+1)` — mixed t,v dependence.
- **#50**: has `v**c4` — power function, not log.

None of these match `log(|v|+1)`.

But more fundamentally, the x-dependence `x*exp(-|x|)` cannot be represented by ANY of these candidates. Every single candidate uses `tanh(c1*x + c2)` (possibly plus `c*x` or `log(c*x²+1)` or `x*exp(...)` terms) for x-dependence. None of these can reproduce `x*exp(-|x|)` for all x values.

Let me double-check candidates with `exp` involving x:
- **#36**: `c3*exp(c4*x)` — this is exponential in x, not `x*exp(-|x|)`.

And candidates with `x**(c)`:
- **#31**: `c3*x**c4` — power of x, not `x*exp(-|x|)`.

None of these functional forms can match `x*exp(-|x|)` for all x.
